1A-   PG 5819— 431 (04/2022)
THE CUSTOM ORDINANCE
Order under Section 19(A)
BY VIRTUE of the power vested in me under Section 19(A) of the Customs Ordinance (Chapter 235), as amended by the 
Customs (Amendment) Law No. 35 of 1974 and the Customs (Amendment) Act, No. 83 of 1988, I, Basil Rajapaksa, Minister 
Column V of the Schedule hereto, imported by or consigned to, 
Column II of that Schedule from payment of the Customs Import 
Column VIII of that Schedule subject to such conditions.
of the Director General of Customs and pay the Customs Import Duty payable on such goods at the time of sale or disposal 
to the Director General of Customs in terms of Section 19 (A) ( 3). Any goods sold or disposed of in contravention of such 
Section shall be liable to be forfeited.
,
Minister of Finance.
Ministry of Finance,
Colombo 01,
25th March, 2022.
